================================================================================
SECTION 6: SUMMARY
================================================================================

FO76 source: 1 files (1st person only)
Fan mod: 52 1P + 12 3P + 7 PA-1P + 4 PA-3P files
Exact filename matches: 1
FO76 has only wpnreload.hkx; fan mod has 52 1P animations

Key observation: FO76 Gauss Shotgun extraction yielded only 1 animation file
while the fan mod created 52 from scratch or adapted from other weapons.
This means the fan mod contains largely ORIGINAL animations, not direct conversions.
